Offset	=2C0
Width	=01

MFG Default	=[01]MITT 
Options	=[00]WITT	// Move "*" to the desired Option
         *[01]MITT

Offset	=2C1
Width	=01

MFG Default	=[00]Disabled 
Options	=*[00]Disabled	// Move "*" to the desired Option
         [01]Enabled - UART0
         [02]Enabled - UART1
         [03]Enabled - UART2
